SoCal Barber needs to be your go-to barbershop in the Norwalk-Downey Community.  The owners opened their brand-new shop with a mission and passion to give the highest quality cuts to their customers.  I can attest that this shop will not disappoint, the customer service sets the highest standard of what competing barber shops should offer.  With more than seven seats and a talented barber to fill each one, you will never have to wait long and will leave looking your absolute freshest. With more than thirty combined years of barbershop experience, the owners strive to give the BEST cuts to their customers.

The shop is modern and welcoming; you immediately walk in to a row of brand new seats, husky toolboxes, and big screen TVs.  The magic is in the details as each barber apron adorns the SoCal logo.

SoCal Barber easily rates a 5 out of 5 for customer service, the owner has a motto that everyone should be treated as family; each customer is offered a bottle of water.

SoCal treats military and first responders very well

Bottom line or TLDR:  This is the best new barbershop in town.  I receive a high quality cut every single week, the price is competitive, the barbers are talented, and the customer service is on point.  Look no further, this is the one.

<Text>I came mostly to boulder but I wound up using a lot of the gym equipment as well.

As far as bouldering goes, there's a pretty small area for it. However, I will say their problems (routes) are fairly difficult. It was much closer to international standards in terms of ratings.

They definitely have their share of top rope, which looked equally difficult, and gym equipment. They have most of what a traditional gym has. There is also more equipment to use in that area. I took advantage of most of their offers and was not disappointed

They do not have air conditioning so it can get fairly hot for those not used to it. but aside from that the facility has good maintenance, is clean, and has a great staff.

TLDR: good climbing gym, lots of weights and other gym equipment. Clean well maintained facility. Stay hydrated.<//Text>< pics>

Although the gym is decent and there's a great community of climbers the owner of the gym is nothing but money hungry. I had a membership for 2 years. During the first year of my membership they were running  a promotion that any money spent at the shop would give you 10 % cash back when you renewed your year membership. Well the year came and went and when I asked about the promotion I was told that they don't do that anymore. I was never given noticed about the discontinuation of the promotion and never received cashed back from the shop.

Another issue with the money grab is I right before I canceled my membership the prices were increased for new customers. I was given a noticed by email that the prices were going to be raised but if you were an old member you were grandfathered in, expect despite being a member for almost two years my membership was still increased.

And finally the state of the gym is a joke. If it wasn't for the fact that they had some decent (and only some decent) setters then it would be a complete joke. I can't count how many times I have come across a spinning hold (and I'm a small person, only 107lbs) or how many times the water fountain has broken and not been fixed. The owner invested in a pathetic Ninja Warrior Course (that guess what you have to pay extra on your membership to use) instead of adding showers to the gym like he said he would.  The owner just obviously has no idea how to run gym. And if that wasn't enough he went and bought another gym to ruin (The Wall Climbing Gym). < text>
Checked out the place yesterday. It'd be a cool gym under normal circumstances, but their COVID protocols are suspect. The place is supposed to be an "open air" facility but the side bay doors were closed. Climbers, basketball players and folks using the weight room weren't wearing masks.

I understand that the current COVID policies allow for some flexibility, but in mind there is absolutely no reason to have maskless climbers and weightlifters - even if you are actually "open air". The risk is too high. Personally, visitors should at all times be wearing masks given that they are breathing all over the holds, walls, etc. I also thought the management could have done a better job spreading more hand sanitizer around the facility, and I didn't see staff wiping down equipment or members for that matter.

For what it's worth, I've been to other climbing gyms during this pandemic that have much better COVID policies, including all visitors having to wear mask and having to clean up after themselves. I have a buddy that manages a climbing gym up in Seattle and it doesn't take that much extra work to require and enforce a solid mask and cleanliness policy.

Oh... might also be worth mentioning that I'm not writing this out of jest. I spent a bunch of time observing everything in hopes of convincing myself that this place would be COVID safe since it's so close to my new home. Sadly not so.</text>

This place has numerous problems and fails to address most of them.

It is designed so you dont cancel while they hold all your bank account info. I mean come on, why else wouldn't an employee of said business be able to cancel an account? They can create them though of course. Absolute money grab.

The owner is rude and impersonal. I was a member there for over a year and the owner would play games on who he likes and doesnt like. If you aren't in the "in" crowd there, expect to be looked down upon by certain staff.

That being said, the facility is dirty and insanely hot. Why climb outside in beautiful socal when you can climb indoors here at 90-100 degrees. They have no ac. The place is a sweatbox. It creates situations that are entirely unsafe for anyone trying to exert themselves to the fullest.
The bathrooms are always broken, and things take forever to actually be fixed. No showers.

The money being spent is spent in all the wrong  places. Really they are being spent for the owner's selfish reasons. The gym desperately needed new gym holds or ac or showers or to fix all the broken stuff around but he instead decided to spend that money on an extremely overpriced "ninja warrior" course that you could build ina few days in your backyard. The owner here does not care about its members. Nor its staff. People are expendable here. There is no love, kindness or personal touches to this place. Toxic. Stay away.< /Review>

Patrice Sabordo< /username>
< Review>
A pretty solid gym! Rock Fitness has great facilities and an excellent top rope and bouldering section. It's nice to have the option to switch from climbing to using the fitness equipment or basketball court throughout the day. There is a crate-stacking activity that climbers can try out and it seems challenging but really fun! Also, it's open 24 hours which is a plus for those who want to get some late-night exercise or climbing in. However, there is a safety concern. Since there is so much variety in terms of what you want to do at the gym and because it's a very family-friendly place, there are a lot of children (and adults) using equipment that they may not know how to operate. At that time, many children were running around and playing on fitness equipment that they should never be in contact with. During the daytime, there weren't enough employees supervising and walking around making sure that people were being safe. Overall though, Rock Fitness is a great facility with friendly employees and I will definitely be returning to the gym!< /Review>

<text>I go to a climbing gym 5-6 times a week in utah, and have now visited this gym twice while in town visiting family. Not a huge climbing gym, but prices are very reasonable for the amount of variety it offers. I had a good experience the first time last year so I decided to bring my rather large family with me the second time taking advantage of their $10 Friday night deal, which really is a steal.

I will preface my justification for the 3 star rating by saying I am sure my group was a nightmare for the staff and other climbers, because we had several young climbers. I have removed one star from my rating because there were no top roping routes that were for climbers at an introductory level with limited athletic ability. At the gym I am sitting at right now I can count 10 top roping routes that are easier than the easiest route they had at rock fitness. Granted the gym I am at is twice the size, but still. When I pointed this out to one of the staff, he directed me to a small bouldering wall, which could occupy someone for maybe 3 minutes, and of course the gym I am at now has a comparable wall about 8 times the size. I realize that wall space is precious, but I am just recommending one or two routes be placed that anyone who can climb a ladder can climb, just to help people build confidence. If you guys choose not to do this, I would recommend improving the communication when people call talking about bringing the un-initiated and young children.

I have deducted another star because several of my family members found the staff unfriendly. I did not feel the same way personally, but I might just have different expectations for climbing gym staff, spending more time at other gyms.

So at the end of the day, while I would for sure sign up myself for this gym if I lived nearby, I would not introduce anyone to climbing through this gym again.<//text><Rating>3</Rating>< Response>

< Review>
If you love fried chicken as much as i do, Popeyes is my No. 1 choice!  Why?  Its perfectly seasoned, not super salty like the others,  battered lightly & tastes so fresh & juicy, underneath its crunchy, golden fried batter.  We have one location here in El Cajon, CA, and always steady  busy, wc is a good indicator that the product is good, as well as the service.  The Staff is very accommodating, pleasant, always a smile & " thank you" for me.  It would do them well to update the image of their store, could use a fresh coat of paint inside & out, clean up landscaping, re-stripe parking lot, fix broken signs & displays outside, clean up drive thru (paint,  wash windows, remove debris from drive way).  It doesn't take much expense plus elbow grease to make this store spiffy & shine. Which goes w the dining room & restrooms inside.  A clean store represents a very good & successful operating  food business, wc draws more patronage.< /Review>
